  // add 'tap' event listener, that opens info bubble, to the group
  group.addEventListener('tap', function (evt) {
    // event target is the marker itself, group is a parent event target
    // for all objects that it contains
    var bubble =  new H.ui.InfoBubble(evt.target.getPosition(), {
      // read custom data
      content: evt.target.getData()
    });
    
    // hide all visible bubbles
    ui.getBubbles().forEach(function(bub){
        ui.removeBubble(bub)
    });
    // show info bubble
    ui.addBubble(bubble);
  }, false);
map.addObject( group );
map.setViewBounds(group.getBounds());

}
addMarkersToMap(map)

        $(function(){
            // Try to show the share buttons in the popup
            $(".share-buttons .window").not('[data-is-email="true"]').click(function(){
                var href=$(this).prop('href');

                var new_window = window.open(href, 'newwindow', 'width=575,height=480,top=' + ((window.innerHeight - 575) / 2) + ', left=' + ((window.innerWidth - 480) / 2) + ',toolbar=no, location=no, directories=no, status=no, menubar=no');

                if($(this).data('isEmail')){
                    new_window.close();
                }

                return false;
            });
        });
